search_repository(repo, max_retries=2):\n"""Search a repository with error handling and retry logic"""\nresults = []\nprint(f"\\n--- Searching {repo[\'name\']} ---")\nfor term in repo[\'terms\']:\nprint(f"Query: {term}")\ntry:\nsearch_url = repo[\'search_url\'].format(query=quote(term))\nprint(f"URL: {search_url[:80]}...")\nfor attempt in range(max_retries):\ntry:\nresponse = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\nprint(f" Attempt {attempt+1}: Status {response.status_code}")\nif response.status_code == 200:\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\nresult_patterns = [\n{\'selector\': \'div.search-result\', \'title\': \'h3, h2, .title\', \'link\': \'a\'},\n{\'selector\': \'.result-item\', \'title\': \'.title, h3, h2\', \'link\': \'a\'},\n{\'selector\': \'article\', \'title\': \'h1, h2, h3, .title\', \'link\': \'a\'},\n{\'selector\': \'.document\', \'title\': \'.title, h3\', \'link\': \'a\'},\n{\'selector\': \'.record\', \'title\': \'.title, h3\', \'link\': \'a\'}\n]\nfound_results = []\nfor pattern in result_patterns:\nelements = soup.select(pattern[\'selector\'])\nif elements:\nprint(f" Found {len(elements)} results title\'\nlink_elem = elem.select_one(pattern[\'link\'])\nif link_elem and link_elem.get(\'href\'):\nlink = link_elem[\'href\']\nif link.startswith(\'/\'):\nlink = urljoin(repo[\'base_url\'], link)\nelse:\nlink = \'\'\nsnippet = elem.get_text().strip()[:300]\ntext_combined = (title + \' \' + snippet).lower()\nrelevance = 0\nif \'federico lauria\' in text_combined:\nrelevance += 15\nelif += 5\nif \'2014\' in text_combined:\nrelevance += 5\nif any(word in text_combined for word in [\'dissertation\', \'thesis\', \'phd\', \'doctoral\']):\nrelevance += 8\nif any(word in text_combined for word in [\'desire\', \'intentionality\', \'deontic\']):\nrelevance += 5\nif relevance > 5: # Only keep relevant results\nfound_results.append({\n\'title\': title,\n\'link\': link,\n\'snippet\': (Score: {found_results[0][\'relevance\']})")\nelse:\nprint(" No relevant results found")\nbreak # Success, no need to retry\nelif response.status_code == 403:\nprint(f" 403 Forbidden - trying again with delay")\ntime.sleep(5)\nelse:\nprint(f" HTTP {response.status_code} - retrying")\ntime.sleep(2)\nexcept requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:\nprint(f" Request error: {str(e)[:100]}")\ntime.sleep(3)\nexcept Exception as e:\nprint(f" Error searching {repo[\'name\']}: {str(e)}")\ntime.sleep(2) # Look for any artwork links or patterns\n        artwork_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True)\n        artwork_patterns = []\n        \n        for link in artwork_links:\n            href = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n            if any(pattern in href for pattern in [\'/artwork/\', \'/object/\', \'/collection-item/\']):\n                artwork_patterns.append({\n                    \'href\': href,\n                    \'text\': link.get_text().strip()[:100]\n                })\n        \n        print(f\'Found {len(artwork_patterns)} potential artwork link patterns:\')\n        for i, pattern in enumerate(artwork_patterns[:10], 1):\n            print(f\'  {i}. {pattern["href"]} -> "{pattern["text"]}"\')\n        \n        # Look for any elements with artwork-related attributes\n            artwork_attrs = soup.find_all(attrs={\'data-artwork\': True})\n            object_attrs = soup.find_all(attrs={\'data-object\': True})\n            \n            print(f\'  Elements with data-artwork: {len(artwork_attrs)}\')\n            print(f\'  Elements with data-object: {len(object_attrs)}\')\n            \n            # Check for JavaScript-loaded content indicators\n            scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\')\n            js_indicators = []\n            for script in scripts:\n                script_text = script.get_text() if script.string else \'\'\n                if any(indicator in script_text.lower() for indicator in [\'ajax\', \'fetch\', \'xhr\', \'api\', \'json\']):\n                    js_indicators.append(script_text[:200] + \'...\' if len(script_text) > 200 else script_text)\n            \n            print(f\'  JavaScript indicators found: {len(js_indicators)}\')\n            if js_indicators:\n                print(\'  Sample JS content:\')\n                for js in js_indicators[:2]:\n                    print(f\'    {js[:150]}...\')\n            \n            # Look for any actual artwork titles or artist names\n            text_content = soup.get_text().lower()\n            potential_titles = []\n            \n            # Common art-related words that might indicate actual content\n            art_indicators = [\'oil on canvas\', \'acrylic\', \'watercolor\', \'sculpture\', \'bronze\', \'marble\', \'untitled\', \'portrait of\', \'landscape\', \'still life\']\n            found_indicators = [indicator for indicator in art_indicators if indicator in text_content]\n            \n            print(f\'  Art medium/type indicators found: {found_indicators}\')\n            \n            # Check if this might be a single-page application (SPA)\n            spa_indicators = [\'react\', \'vue\', \'angular\', \'app.js\', \'bundle.js\']\n            spa_found = [indicator for indicator in spa_indicators if indicator in text_content]\n            \n            print(f\'  SPA framework indicators: {spa_found}\')\n            \n            # Save analysis\n            analysis = {\n                \'search_term\': term,\n                \'url\': search_url,\n                \'status_code\': response.status_code,\n                \'containers_found\': containers_found,\n                \'artwork_attrs_count\': len(artwork_attrs),\n                \'object_attrs_count\': len(object_attrs),\n                \'js_indicators_count\': len(js_indicators),\n                \'art_indicators_found\': found_indicators,\n                \'spa_indicators_found\': spa_found,\n                \'page_text_length\': len(text_content),\n                \'analysis_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\')\n            }\n            \n            with open(f\'workspace/search_analysis_{i}_{term}.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                json.dump(analysis, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n            \n            print(f\'  Analysis saved to: workspace/search_analysis_{i}_{term}.json\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'  Search failed: HTTP {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  Error with test search "{term}": {str(e)}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(2)\n\nprint(\'\\n=== STEP 2: EXPLORING ALTERNATIVE SAAM ACCESS METHODS ===\')\n\n# Try the Smithsonian API if available\nprint(\'\\n--- Attempting Smithsonian Open Access API ---\')\nsi_api_base = \'https://api.si.edu/openaccess/api/v1.0\'\napi_search_url = f\'{si_api_base}/search\'\n\ntry:\n    # Extract relevant information\n                if \'response\' in api_data and \'rows\' in api_data[\'response\']:\n                    rows = api_data[\'response\'][\'rows\']\n                    print(f\'  Found {len(rows)} results for "{term}"\')\n                    \n                    for i, row in enumerate(rows[:3], 1):\n                        title = row.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                        content = row.get(\'content\', {})\n                        descriptiveNonRepeating = content.get(\'descriptiveNonRepeating\', {})\n                        \n                        unit_code = descriptiveNonRepeating.get(\'unit_code\', \'\')\n                        if unit_code == \'SAAM\':  #
